<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p90 ft5">Exchange of information upon request</P>
<P class="p91 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">The competent authority of the requested Party shall provide upon request information for the purposes referred to in Article 1. Such information shall be exchanged without regard to whether the conduct being investigated would constitute a crime under the laws of the requested Party if such conduct occurred in the requested Party.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p92 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft8">If the information in the possession of the competent authority of the requested Party is not sufficient to enable it to comply with the request for information, the requested Party shall use all relevant information gathering measures to provide the applicant Party with the information requested, notwithstanding that the requested Party may not need such information for its own tax purposes.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p93 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">If specifically requested by the competent authority of the applicant Party, the competent authority of the requested Party shall provide information under this Article, to the extent allowable under its domestic laws, in the form of depositions of witnesses and authenticated copies of original records.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p92 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">Each Party shall ensure that its competent authority, for the purposes of this Agreement, has the authority to obtain and provide</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p94 ft5">Utbyte av upplysningar p√• beg√§ran</P>
<P class="p95 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">Den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den anmodade parten ska p√• beg√§ran l√§mna upplysningar f√∂r de √§ndam√•l som anges i artikel 1. <P class="p96 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Om de upplysningar som √§r tillg√§ngliga f√∂r den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den anmodade parten inte r√§cker till f√∂r att tillm√∂tesg√• en beg√§ran om upplysningar, ska den anmodade parten ‚Äì utan hinder av att den anmodade parten kanske inte har behov av upplysningarna f√∂r sina egna beskattnings√§ndam√•l ‚Äì utnyttja alla relevanta √•tg√§rder f√∂r att inh√§mta upplysningarna till den anmodande parten.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p97 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">Om den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den anmodande parten s√§rskilt beg√§r det, ska den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den anmodade parten ‚Äì i den utstr√§ckning som detta √§r till√•tet enligt dess interna lagstiftning ‚Äì l√§mna upplysningar enligt denna artikel i form av upptagande av vittnesber√§ttelser och bestyrkta kopior av handlingar.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p97 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft22">Vardera parten ska s√§kerst√§lla att dess beh√∂riga myndighet, f√∂r till√§mpningen av detta avtal, har</SPAN></P>

<P class="p15 ft2">upon request:</P>
<P class="p98 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">information held by banks, other financial institutions, and any person, including nominees and trustees, acting in an agency or fiduciary capacity;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p99 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft31">information regarding the</SPAN></P>
<P class="p100 ft2">ownership of companies, partnerships and other persons, including, within the constraints of Article 2, ownership information on all such persons in an ownership chain; in the case of trusts, information on settlors, trustees, beneficiaries and the position in an ownership chain; and in the case of foundations, information on founders, members of the foundation council and beneficiaries and the position in an ownership chain.</P>
<P class="p101 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">This Agreement does not create an obligation on the Parties to obtain or provide:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p102 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">ownership information with respect to publicly traded companies or public collective investment funds or schemes unless such information can be obtained without giving rise to disproportionate difficulties;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p103 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">information relating to a period more than six years prior to the tax period under consideration;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p104 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft33">information unless the applicant Party has pursued all means available in its own Party to obtain the information, except those that would give rise to disproportionate difficulties;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p105 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">information in the possession of or obtainable by a person other than the taxpayer that does not directly relate to the taxpayer.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p15 ft23">Article 11</P>
<P class="p135 ft5">No prejudicial or restrictive measures</P>
<P class="p136 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">In the event that a Party has reason to believe that the other Party has introduced prejudicial or restrictive measures based on harmful tax practices to residents or nationals of the other Party, both Parties shall immediately initiate competent authority proceedings to resolve the matter.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p137 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft30">A prejudicial or restrictive measure based on harmful tax practices means a measure applied by one Party to residents or nationals of either Party on the basis that the other Party does not engage in effective exchange of information or because it lacks transparency in the operation of its laws, regulations or administrative practices, or on the basis of no or nominal taxes and one of the preceding criteria.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p138 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft39">Without limiting the generality of the term ‚Äúprejudicial</SPAN></P>
</DIV>

<P class="p84 ft2">PROTOCOL TO THE AGREE- MENT BETWEEN THE KING- DOM OF SWEDEN AND BERMUDA (AS AUTHORISED BY THE UNITED KINGDOM OF GREAT BRITAIN AND NORTHERN IRELAND) ON THE EXCHANGE OF INFOR- MATION WITH RESPECT TO TAXES</P>
<P class="p152 ft2">At the moment of signing the Agreement on the exchange of information with respect to taxes between the Kingdom of Sweden and Bermuda, the Parties have agreed that the following provisions shall form an integral part of the Agreement:</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p84 ft2">PROTOKOLL TILL AVTALET MELLAN KONUNGARIKET SVERIGE OCH BERMUDA (ENLIGT BEMYNDIGANDE</P>
<P class="p153 ft2">FR√ÖN DET F√ñRENADE KONUNGARIKET STORBRI- TANNIEN OCH NORDIRLAND) OM UTBYTE AV UPPLYS- NINGAR AVSEENDE SKAT- TER</P>
<P class="p154 ft6">Vid undertecknandet av avtalet om utbyte av upplysningar avseende skatter mellan Konungariket Sverige och Bermuda, har parterna kommit √∂verens om att f√∂ljande best√§mmelser ska utg√∂ra en integrerande del av avtalet:</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">

	<TD class="tr3 td109"><SPAN class="p18 ft3">I. Allm√§nt</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<DIV id="id_4">
<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p134 ft2">The Government of Bermuda will take the measures necessary to repeal any provision of its domestic legislation that requires that information is physically present for the purposes of fulfilling the Agreement. The Government of Sweden in turn will pursue all means available in its own territory to obtain the information, except those that would give rise to disproportionate difficulties.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4_2">
<P class="p134 ft2">Bermudas regering ska vidta n√∂dv√§ndiga √•tg√§rder f√∂r att upph√§va varje best√§mmelse i sin inhemska lagstiftning som kr√§ver att upplysningar m√•ste finnas fysiskt tillg√§ngliga i syfte att uppfylla avtalet. <P class="p15 ft23">Article 3</P>
<P class="p190 ft5">Principles applying to the adjustment of profits of associated enterprises</P>

<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p15 ft3">Mutual agreement procedures</P>
<P class="p197 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Where an enterprise considers that, in any case to which this Agreement applies, the principles set out in Article 3 have not been observed, it may, irrespective of the remedies provided by the domestic law of the Party concerned, present its case to the competent authority of the Party of which it is a resident. The case must be presented within three years from the first notification of the action which is contrary or is likely to be contrary to the principles set out in Article 3. The competent authority shall then without delay notify the competent authority of the other Party.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p198 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft21">The competent authority shall endeavour, if the objection appears to it to be justified and if it is not itself able to arrive at a satisfactory solution, to resolve the case by mutual agreement with the competent authority of the other Party, with a view to the avoidance of taxation which is not in accordance with the Agreement. Any agreement reached shall be implemented notwithstanding any time limits in the domestic law of the Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p101 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft34">The competent authorities of the Parties shall endeavour to resolve by mutual agreement any difficulties or doubts arising as to the interpretation or application of the Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft50"><SPAN class="ft50">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft51">The competent authorities of</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">

<P class="p201 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">Om den beh√∂riga myndigheten finner inv√§ndningen grundad men inte sj√§lv kan f√• till st√•nd en tillfredsst√§llande l√∂sning, ska den beh√∂riga myndigheten s√∂ka avg√∂ra saken genom en √∂msesidig √∂verenskommelse med den beh√∂riga myndigheten i den andra parten i syfte att undvika beskattning som strider mot avtalet. √ñverenskommelse som tr√§ffas genomf√∂rs utan hinder av tidsgr√§nser i parternas interna lagstiftning.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p84 ft6">provisions of paragraph 1 an individual is a resident of both Parties, then his status shall be determined as follows:</P>

<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p15 ft23">Article 5</P>
<P class="p139 ft3">Income from employment</P>
<P class="p230 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft29">Subject to the provisions of Articles 6, 7, 8 and 9, salaries, wages and other similar remuneration derived by a resident of a Party in respect of an employment shall be taxable only in that Party unless the employment is exercised in the other Party. If the employment is so exercised, such remuneration as is derived therefrom may be taxed in that other Party.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p231 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft56">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 1, remuneration derived by a resident of a Party in respect of an employment exercised in the other Party shall be taxable only in the first-</SPAN></P>

<P class="p15 ft23">Article 12</P>
<P class="p139 ft3">Mutual agreement procedure</P>
<P class="p243 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft21">Where an individual considers that the actions of one or both of the Parties result or will result for him in taxation not in accordance with the provisions of this Agreement, he may, irrespective of the remedies provided by the domestic law of those Parties, present his case to the competent authority of the Party of which he is a resident. <P class="p268 ft18">4.1 Lagf√∂rslaget</P>
<P class="p269 ft6">I f√∂rslaget till lag f√∂reskrivs att avtalet ska g√§lla som lag h√§r i landet. Avtalet √§r uppr√§ttat p√• engelska. Avtalstexten och en svensk √∂vers√§ttning framg√•r av bilagan till lagen.</P>
<P class="p167 ft6">Enligt artikel 13 i avtalet ska parterna underr√§tta varandra n√§r de √•tg√§rder vidtagits som kr√§vs f√∂r att avtalet ska tr√§da i kraft. Det √§r s√•ledes inte m√∂jligt att nu avg√∂ra vid vilken tidpunkt avtalet kommer att tr√§da i kraft. <P class="p270 ft18">4.2 Informationsutbytesavtalets inneh√•ll</P>
<P class="p271 ft2">Avtalet ansluter n√§ra till OECD:s (Organisationen f√∂r ekonomiskt samarbete och utveckling) modellavtal f√∂r informationsutbyte i skatte√§renden (Agreement on Exchange of Information on Tax Matters, modellavtalet), vilket utarbetats inom ramen f√∂r OECD:s arbete mot skadliga skatteregimer. I OECD:s rapport Harmful Tax Competition: An Emerging Global Issue, 1998, anges avsaknad av effektivt informationsutbyte som ett huvudkriterium f√∂r s.k. skadliga skatteregimer.
